; Intermission texts

> E1TEXT
; Doom Ep.1
"""Once you beat the big badasses and
clean out the moon base you're supposed
to win, aren't you? Aren't you? Where's
your fat reward and ticket home? What
the hell is this? It's not supposed to
end this way!

It stinks like rotten meat, but looks
like the lost Deimos base. Looks like
you're stuck on The Shores of Hell.
The only way out is through.

To continue the DOOM experience, play
The Shores of Hell and its amazing
sequel, Inferno!
"""
"""一旦你打败那些大坏蛋，清理完月球基地，
你就该赢了，不是吗？不是吗？
你的丰厚奖赏和回家的票呢？
这到底是怎么回事？不该这样结束的！

这里臭气熏天，像腐肉一样，
但看起来像是失落的火卫一基地。
看来你被困在地狱海岸了。
唯一的出路就是向前冲。

要继续《DOOM》的体验，
就玩《地狱海岸》
及其精彩的续作《炼狱》！
"""

> E2TEXT
; Doom Ep.2
"""You've done it! The hideous cyber-
demon lord that ruled the lost Deimos
moon base has been slain and you
are triumphant! But ... where are
you? You clamber to the edge of the
moon and look down to see the awful
truth.

Deimos floats above Hell itself!
You've never heard of anyone escaping
from Hell, but you'll make the bastards
sorry they ever heard of you! Quickly,
you rappel down to the surface of
Hell.

Now, it's on to the final chapter of
DOOM! -- Inferno."""
"""你成功了！统治着失落的迪莫斯月球
基地的丑恶机械巨魔领主已被消灭，
你取得了胜利！但是……你在哪里？
你爬到月球边缘向下望去，看到了可怕的真相。

迪莫斯竟漂浮在地狱之上！
你从未听说过有人能从地狱逃脱，
但你会让那些混蛋后悔认识你！
你迅速用绳索滑降到地狱表面。

现在，是时候开启《DOOM》的
最终篇章——《炼狱》了。"""

> E3TEXT
; Doom Ep.3
"""The loathsome spiderdemon that
masterminded the invasion of the moon
bases and caused so much death has had
its ass kicked for all time.

A hidden doorway opens and you enter.
You've proven too tough for Hell to
contain, and now Hell at last plays
fair -- for you emerge from the door
to see the green fields of Earth!
Home at last.

You wonder what's been happening on
Earth while you were battling evil
unleashed. It's good that no Hell-
spawn could have come through that
door with you ..."""
"""那个策划了月球基地入侵并造成无数
死亡的可恶蜘蛛恶魔已被永远击败。

一道隐藏的门打开了，你走了进去。
你证明了自己强大到地狱都无法再将你囚禁，
现在地狱终于公平行事——
因为你从门里出来，
看到了地球那片绿色的田野！终于回家了。

你好奇在你与邪恶势力战斗期间
地球上发生了什么。
好在没有地狱的恶魔
能和你一起从那扇门出来……"""

> E4TEXT
; Doom Ep.4
"""The spider mastermind must have sent forth
its legions of hellspawn before your
final confrontation with that terrible
beast from hell. but you stepped forward
and brought forth eternal damnation and
suffering upon the horde as a true hero
would in the face of something so evil.

Besides, someone was gonna pay for what
happened to Daisy, your pet rabbit.

But now, you see spread before you more
potential pain and gibbitude as a nation
of demons run amok among our cities.

Next stop, Hell on Earth!"""
"""蜘蛛首脑肯定在你与那来自地狱的可怕野兽的
最终对决之前就已派出大批地狱恶灵。
但你挺身而出，像真正的英雄那样，
给这群恶魔带来了永恒的诅咒和折磨。

而且，总得有人为黛西——
你的宠物兔子——所遭受的一切付出代价。

但现在，你面前展现的是更多的痛苦和残杀，
恶魔大军在我们的城市中肆虐横行。

下一站，《人间地狱》！"""

> C1TEXT
; Doom2 after MAP06
"""You have entered deeply into the infested
starport. But something is wrong. The
monsters have brought their own reality
with them, and the starport's technology
is being subverted by their presence.

Ahead, you see an outpost of hell, a
fortified zone. If you can get past it,
You can penetrate into the haunted heart
of the starbase and find the controlling
switch which holds earth's population
hostage."""
"""你已深入被怪物侵扰的星际港。
但情况不对劲。怪物带来了它们自己的现实，
它们的存在正在颠覆星际港的技术。

前方，你看到一片地狱的前哨，一个设防区域。
若能突破它，你就能深入到被诅咒的星港核心，
找到控制着地球人口命运的开关。"""

> C2TEXT
; Doom2 after MAP11
"""You have won! Your victory has enabled
Humankind to evacuate earth and escape
the nightmare. Now you are the only
Human left on the face of the planet.
Cannibal mutations, carnivorous aliens,
and evil spirits are your only neighbors.
You sit back and wait for death, content
that you have saved your species.

But then, Earth Control beams down a
message from space: "Sensors have located
the source of the alien invasion. If you
go there, you may be able to block their
entry. The alien base is in the heart of
your own home city, not far from the
starport." Slowly and painfully you get
up and return to the fray."""
"""你赢了！你的胜利让人类得以撤离地球，逃离噩梦。
如今你是这颗星球上唯一的人类。
食人变异体、食肉外星人和恶灵是你唯一的邻居。
你坐等死亡，心满意足于自己拯救了人类。

但随后，地球控制中心从太空传来了信息：
“传感器已定位到外星入侵的源头。
如果你们前往那里，或许能够阻止他们的入侵。
外星基地就在你们自己的城市中心，
离星际港不远。”
你艰难而痛苦地起身，重新投入战斗。"""

> C3TEXT
; Doom 2 after MAP20
"""You are at the corrupt heart of the city,
surrounded by the corpses of your enemies.
You see no way to destroy the creatures'
entryway on this side, so you clench your
teeth and plunge through it.

There must be a way to close it on the
other side. What do you care if you've
got to go through hell to get to it?"""
"""你身处这座城市的腐败中心，四周都是敌人的尸体。
你发现无法摧毁这边怪物的入口，
于是咬紧牙关，纵身一跃冲了进去。

在另一边肯定有办法把它关上。
就算得穿过地狱才能到达，你又何必在意？"""

> C4TEXT
; Doom2 victory
"""The horrendous visage of the biggest
demon you've ever seen crumbles before
you, after you pump your rockets into
his exposed brain. The monster shrivels
up and dies, its thrashing limbs
devastating untold miles of hell's
surface.

You've done it. The invasion is over.
Earth is saved. Hell is a wreck. You
wonder where bad folks will go when they
die, now. Wiping the sweat from your
forehead you begin the long trek back
home. Rebuilding earth ought to be a
lot more fun than ruining it was.
"""
"""你朝那颗暴露在外的大脑猛射火箭弹，
眼前出现的那张你所见过的
最大的恶魔的可怕面孔瞬间崩塌。
那怪物萎缩着死去，它抽搐的四肢
毁掉了地狱表面无数英里的土地。

你做到了。入侵结束了。
地球得救了。地狱一片狼藉。
你不禁好奇，现在坏人死后会去往何处。
擦去额头上的汗水，你踏上了漫长的归家之路。
重建地球应该比毁坏它有趣得多。
"""

struggles will have been wasted. Keep
moving, keep fighting, keep killing.
Oh yes, keep living, too."""

夺回了加速器。你放松下来，环顾四周。
该死！本应至少有一台能用的原型机，
可你却看不到。肯定是恶魔们把它拿走了。

你必须找到原型机，否则你所有的努力都将白费。
继续前进，继续战斗，继续杀戮。
哦，对了，也要继续活下去。"""

> HE1TEXT

Those creatures had to come from
somewhere, though, and you have the
sneaky suspicion that the fiery
portal of hell's maw opens onto

To make sure that more undead

through, you'll have to seal Hell's
maw from the other side. Of course
this means you may get stuck in a
very unfriendly world, but no one
ever said being a heretic was easy!"""
"""随着铁冰霜巨龙巫妖及其爪牙的覆灭，
这方位面存在的最后一批亡灵已被肃清。

那些生物总得来自某个地方，
而你隐隐觉得，
地狱之口那熊熊燃烧的传送门，
正通往它们的家园所在维度。

为了确保不会有更多不死生物
（甚至更糟糕的东西）涌出，
你得从另一边封住地狱之口。
当然，这意味着你可能会被困在
一个非常不友好的世界里，
但从来没人说过当异教徒是件容易的事！"""

> HE2TEXT

overhead where the sky should be is

他们守卫的门户已然开启，
露出的正是你所期盼的归家之路。
然而当你迈步踏入，
耳边却回荡着嘲弄的笑声。

难道是别的什么力量在控制着这些牛头怪？
这扇门后面会不会还有更可怕的生物？
头顶上本应是天空的地方却笼罩着
一个水晶穹顶，这显然不是什么好兆头……"""

> HE3TEXT

the magical bonds holding his
creatures on this plane, their
dying screams overwhelming his own
cries of agony.

Your oath of vengeance fulfilled,
you enter the portal to your own
world, mere moments before the dome
shatters into a million pieces.

But if D'Sparil's power is broken
forever, why don't you feel safe?
Was it that last shout just before

; Strife subtitles

> TXT_SUB_INTRO1
; Menu's intro.
The comet struck our planet without warning. We lost our paradise in a single violent stroke.
彗星がこの星に突然衝突した。私達の楽園はこの一撃で失われた。

> TXT_SUB_INTRO2
; 〃
The impact released a virus, which swept through the land and killed millions. They turned out to be the lucky ones.
"""彗星の衝突によりウィルスが世界中に放たれ、数えきれないほどの人々が死んだ。
今から考えれば、彼らはまだ運がいい方だった。"""

> TXT_SUB_INTRO3
; 〃
For those who did not die became mutations of humanity. Some became fanatics who heard the voice of a malignant god in their heads and called themselves "the Order".
"""死ななかった人々は、人間から変異して別の物となった。
一部の人々は、頭の中に邪悪な神の声を伝えられた狂信者となり、
自らの集団を'オーダー'と呼んだ。"""

> TXT_SUB_INTRO4
; 〃
Those of us who are deaf to this voice suffer horribly and are forced to serve these ruthless psychotics who wield weapons more powerful than anything we can muster.
"""その神の声を聞き取れなかった私達は苦しんだ挙げ句、
この無慈悲な狂人どもに仕えるのを強いられた。
そして奴等は、私達のどんな武器とも比べ物にならないほど強力な兵器を持っているのだ。"""

> TXT_SUB_INTRO5
; 〃
They destroy our women and children so that we must hide them underground and live like animals in constant fear for our lives.
"""奴等は女性や子供を殺害していくため、私達はそういった人々を地下に隠さなければならなかった。
我々は動物のように暮らすのを強いられ、命は常に危険に晒されている。"""

> TXT_SUB_INTRO6
; 〃
But there are whispers of discontent. If we organize, can we defeat our masters? Weapons are being stolen, soldiers are being trained. A movement is born: born of lifelong strife!
"""だが不満のささやきは常にある。もし私達が力を合わせれば、
支配者たちを倒すことができるだろうか? 奴等の武器は盗まれ続けていて、
我らの兵士たちは訓練され続けている。
革命への動きは生まれたのだ- 終わりなき闘争(Strife)から!"""

> TXT_SUB_GOOD1
; Best ending.
Attention, all troops of the Front: he's done it! It's over. Blackbird's soldier has killed the Evil. The Order is no more. Blackbird, do you read me?
"""フロントの兵士たちよ、聞きたまえ! 彼がすべてを終わらせたのだ。
もうこれで何もかも終わりだ。ブラックバードの兵士が悪を滅ぼしたのだ。
オーダーはもう存在しない。ブラックバード、聞こえるか?"""

> TXT_SUB_GOOD2
; 〃
I knew you would win, my gallant hero. All fighting has stopped. Your victory will allow us to create a vaccine to purge the virus from our bodies.
"""あなたが勝つことは分かっていたわ、私の勇敢なヒーロー。
全ての戦いは終結した。あなたがもたらした勝利のおかげで、
私達の体からウィルスを根絶するためのワクチンを作ることができる。"""

> TXT_SUB_GOOD3
; 〃
You have saved our planet and set us free. Now I'd like to thank you... personally. Oh, and by the way: the name is Shauna.
"""あなたはこの星を救い、そして自由を取り戻した。さあ、
あなたにお礼をするときが来たわね、個人的な意味で...
ああ、それはそうと、私の本名はシャウナよ。"""

> TXT_SUB_SAD1
; Sad ending.
Yes, the evil was gone, but our future was uncertain and clouded with doubt.
"""ええ、悪は消え去ったわ。だけども私達の未来は
まだ不安と疑念に満ちている。"""

> TXT_SUB_SAD2
; 〃
It would take generations to purge the virus from our people. If we survived that long.
"""人間たちからウィルスを根絶するには、あと何世代もかかって
しまうはず。私達がそこまで生き延びられたとしても。"""

> TXT_SUB_SAD3
; 〃
Whatever the evil wanted, it drained from us the one thing we needed: it left us without hope.
"""あの邪悪な存在が何を求めていたかはともかく、
奴は人間たちから一番大切な物、希望を奪い去った。"""

> TXT_SUB_BAD1
; Worst ending.
The sentient virus hit us like a tidal wave, driving us all mad. We heard the siren's song of death and we danced.
"""センティエント・ウィルスは私達を津波のように襲い、
全ての人間を狂気に陥れた。セイレーンの死の歌声を聞いたように
なり、死ぬまで踊り続けたのだ。"""

> TXT_SUB_BAD2
; 〃
This evil drained us of all human life and, scornful of procreation, recycled our families.
"""この邪悪な存在は人間たちの命と繁殖能力を奪い去り、
我々の家族を再利用した。"""

> TXT_SUB_BAD3
; 〃
Then one day, the evil left. There was simply nothing for it to feed on. We were extinct.
"""そしてある時、邪悪な存在はこの星を後にした。単に、
奴の糧となる者が一人もいなくなったからだ。我々は滅びたのだ。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP03_1
; MAP03: After destroying the gate controls.
The genetic mutations caused by the virus not only warped the psyches of the Order, but caused their bodies to decay.
"""ウィルスからもたらされた遺伝子変異はオーダーの者たちの精神だけではなく、
肉体すらも蝕んだ。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP03_2
; 〃
Without procreation, the Order found that biomechanical enhancements were the only way to maintain their strengths and numbers.
"""繁殖行為という選択肢がないオーダーは、
彼らのパワーと数を保つには生体工学による人体改造しかないと判断したのだ。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP03_3
; 〃
The decay has advanced so that most of the troops we face are more machine than man but we believe that their collective consciousness is controlled by one source...
"""彼らの肉体へのダメージは深刻で、我らが遭遇した兵士たちは人間と言うよりは
もはや機械に近いと言える。だが、彼らの集合意識はたった一人によってコントロールされていると
我々は考えている。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP03_4
; 〃
...the Programmer: creator of the AI which controls the Acolytes. Destroy the Programmer, and we may cripple the Order's troops with a single blow. But caution: we have reports he can vaporize attackers.
"""その者の名はプログラマーだ。
彼はアコライト達を操作している人工知能の作成者だ。
プログラマーを殺害すれば、それによってオーダーの兵士たちを無力化できるはずだ。
だが気をつけておけ、ヤツは熱で敵を蒸発させられるとの報告があるからな。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP10_1
; MAP10: Macil.
Fragments assembled from the Programmers files tell us that the Order is worshipping an intelligent weapon. They call it "the Sigil".
"""プログラマーの資料を要約するとその欠片はオーダー達が崇拝する知性を持った武器、
'シジル'だ。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP10_2
; 〃
The piece you touched and recovered is one of five. It wields power drawn from the user's own life force. While you live, you control its power.
"""君が欠片を取り戻したがそれは5つある内の1つだ。
使用者の生命を吸い上げ激しい力を引き出す。
ただ制御下におけるのは生きている間だけだ。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP10_3
; 〃
The shock which knocked you out was the Sigil piece tuning itself to you, your pulse and brain waves. You can wield it, but at a cost: it will drain you dry.
"""君を気絶させた衝撃は、シジルの欠片が脈拍と脳波を同期させた際に起こした様だ。
それを振り回す時は気を付けろ、代償で体が干上がってしまうらしい。"""

> TXT_SUB_MAP10_4
; 〃
One piece constitutes awesome power. Possession of all five pieces would be devastating and would give the user total control of the planet.
"""だがたった一つでも相当な力を放つ。
それが5つ揃った時は圧倒的な力で世界をも支配下に置けるだろう。"""

> TXT_SUB_LOG2
; MAP02: After getting the com unit from Rowan and leaving his room.
Listen, this com unit tells me that you're 100% human. I've been ordered to bring you in, we're talking trust here. Betray me and pay. Oh, and by the way, you can call me Blackbird.
"""聞こえるか、この無線機がアナタは100%人間だと判断した。
私はアナタを信頼して良いとみて連れて来るよう命じられた、
反乱への報酬は期待して良いわ。ああ、それと、私の名はブラックバードよ。"""
